##### <a name="7151-bitmapentry2--bitmapentryclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1324">7.1.5.1 BitmapEntry \[ 2 \] ... Campi BitmapEntry \[ ClusterCount+1 \]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1324">7.1.5.1 BitmapEntry\[2\] ... BitmapEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1325">Ogni campo BitmapEntry in questa matrice rappresenta un cluster nell'heap del cluster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1325">Each BitmapEntry field in this array represents a cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1326">BitmapEntry \[ 2 \] rappresenta il primo cluster nell'heap del cluster e BitmapEntry \[ ClusterCount+1 rappresenta \] l'ultimo cluster nell'heap del cluster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1326">BitmapEntry\[2\] represents the first cluster in the Cluster Heap and BitmapEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] represents the last cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1327">I valori validi per questi campi devono essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1327">The valid values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1328">0, che descrive il cluster corrispondente come disponibile per l'allocazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1328">0, which describes the corresponding cluster as available for allocation</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1329">1, che descrive il cluster corrispondente come non disponibile per l'allocazione (un'allocazione del cluster potrebbe già utilizzare il cluster corrispondente o il fat attivo può descrivere il cluster corrispondente come non eroso)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1329">1, which describes the corresponding cluster as not available for allocation (a cluster allocation may already consume the corresponding cluster or the active FAT may describe the corresponding cluster as bad)</span></span>

### <a name="72-up-case-table-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1330">7.2 Voce della directory della tabella up-case</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1330">7.2 Up-case Table Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1331">La tabella Up-case definisce la conversione da caratteri minuscoli a caratteri maiuscoli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1331">The Up-case Table defines the conversion from lower-case to upper-case characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1332">Ciò è importante perché la voce di directory Nome file (vedere la sezione 7.7) usa caratteri Unicode e il file system exFAT non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole e non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1332">This is important due to the File Name directory entry (see Section 7.7) using Unicode characters and the exFAT file system being case insensitive and case preserving.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1333">La tabella Up-case esiste nell'heap del cluster (vedere la sezione [7.2.5)](#725-up-case-table)e ha una voce di directory primaria critica corrispondente nella directory radice (vedere [la tabella 23).](#table-23-up-case-table-directoryentry-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1333">The Up-case Table exists in the Cluster Heap (see [Section 7.2.5](#725-up-case-table)) and has a corresponding critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 23](#table-23-up-case-table-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1334">Il numero valido di voci della directory Tabella maiuscole/minuscole è 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1334">The valid number of Up-case Table directory entries is 1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1335">A causa della relazione tra la tabella Up-case e i nomi di file, le implementazioni non devono modificare la tabella Up-case, tranne in seguito a operazioni di formattazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1335">Due to the relationship between the Up-case Table and file names, implementations should not modify the Up-case Table, except as a result of format operations.</span></span>

#### <a name="722-tablechecksum-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1379">7.2.2 Campo TableChecksum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1379">7.2.2 TableChecksum Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1380">Il campo TableChecksum contiene il checksum della tabella Up-case (descritta dai campi FirstCluster e DataLength).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1380">The TableChecksum field contains the checksum of the Up-case Table (which the FirstCluster and DataLength fields describe).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1381">Le implementazioni verificano che il contenuto di questo campo sia valido prima di usare la tabella Up-case.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1381">Implementations shall verify the contents of this field are valid prior to using the Up-case Table.</span></span>

<div id="figure-3-tablechecksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1382">**Figura 3 Calcolo tableChecksum**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1382">**Figure 3 TableChecksum Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt32 TableChecksum
(
    UCHAR  * Table,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-case table
    UInt64   DataLength
)
{
    UInt32 Checksum = 0;
    UInt64 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < DataLength; Index++)
    {
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x80000000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) + (UInt32)Table[Index];
    }

    return Checksum;
}
```

#### <a name="723-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1383">7.2.3 Campo FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1383">7.2.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1384">Il campo FirstCluster deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (vedere [la sezione 6.3.5).](#635-firstcluster-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1384">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1385">Questo campo contiene l'indice del primo cluster della catena di cluster, come descritto dal fat, che ospita la tabella Up-case.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1385">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Up-case Table.</span></span>

#### <a name="724-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1386">7.2.4 Campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1386">7.2.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1387">Il campo DataCluster deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (vedere [la sezione 6.3.6).](#636-datalength-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1387">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="725-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1388">7.2.5 Tabella up case</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1388">7.2.5 Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1389">Una tabella up-case è una serie di mapping di caratteri Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1389">An up-case table is a series of Unicode character mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1390">Un mapping dei caratteri è costituito da un campo a 2 byte, con l'indice del campo nella tabella maiuscole/minuscole che rappresenta il carattere Unicode di cui eseguire l'up-case e il campo a 2 byte che rappresenta il carattere Unicode con distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1390">A character mapping consists of a 2-byte field, with the index of the field in the up-case table representing the Unicode character to be up-cased, and the 2-byte field representing the up-cased Unicode character.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1391">I primi 128 caratteri Unicode hanno mapping obbligatori (vedere [la tabella 24).](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1391">The first 128 Unicode characters have mandatory mappings (see [Table 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1392">Una tabella up-case con qualsiasi altro mapping di caratteri per i primi 128 caratteri Unicode non è valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1392">An up-case table which has any other character mapping for any of the first 128 Unicode characters is invalid.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1393">Le implementazioni che supportano solo caratteri dell'intervallo di mapping obbligatorio possono ignorare i mapping del resto della tabella up-case.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1393">Implementations which only support characters from the mandatory mapping range may ignore the mappings of the rest of the up-case table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1394">Tali implementazioni devono usare solo caratteri dell'intervallo di mapping obbligatorio durante la creazione o la ridenominazione dei file (tramite la voce di directory Nome file, vedere [la sezione 7.7).](#77-file-name-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1394">Such implementations shall only use characters from the mandatory mapping range when creating or renaming files (via the File Name directory entry, see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1395">Quando si esegue l'up-casing dei nomi di file esistenti, tali implementazioni non devono eseguire l'up-case dei caratteri dell'intervallo di mapping non obbligatorio, ma devono lasciarli intatti nel nome file con distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole risultante (si tratta di un up-casing parziale).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1395">When up-casing existing file names, such implementations shall not up-case characters from the non-mandatory mapping range, but shall leave them intact in the resulting up-cased file name (this is a partial up-casing).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1396">Durante il confronto dei nomi di file, tali implementazioni devono considerare equivalenti i nomi di file che differiscono dal nome confrontato solo con i caratteri Unicode dell'intervallo di mapping non obbligatorio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1396">When comparing file names, such implementations shall treat file names which differ from the name under comparison only by Unicode characters from the non-mandatory mapping range as equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1397">Anche se tali nomi di file sono potenzialmente equivalenti, tali implementazioni non possono garantire che il nome di file completamente con distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole non sia in conflitto con il nome in fase di confronto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1397">While such file names are only potentially equivalent, such implementations cannot ensure the fully up-cased file name does not collide with the name under comparison.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1516">**0060h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1516">**0060h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1517">0060h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1517">0060h</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1518">**0041h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1518">**0041h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1519">**0042h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1519">**0042h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1520">**0043h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1520">**0043h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1521">**0044h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1521">**0044h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1522">**0045h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1522">**0045h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1523">**0046h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1523">**0046h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1524">**0047h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1524">**0047h**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1525">**0068h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1525">**0068h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1526">**0048h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1526">**0048h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1527">**0049h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1527">**0049h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1528">**004Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1528">**004Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1529">**004Bh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1529">**004Bh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1530">**004Ch**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1530">**004Ch**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1531">**004Dh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1531">**004Dh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1532">**004Eh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1532">**004Eh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1533">**004Fh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1533">**004Fh**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1534">**0070h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1534">**0070h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1535">**0050h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1535">**0050h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1536">**0051h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1536">**0051h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1537">**0052h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1537">**0052h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1538">**0053h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1538">**0053h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1539">**0054h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1539">**0054h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1540">**0055h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1540">**0055h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1541">**0056h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1541">**0056h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1542">**0057h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1542">**0057h**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1543">**0078h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1543">**0078h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1544">**0058h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1544">**0058h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1545">**0059h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1545">**0059h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1546">**005Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1546">**005Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1547">007Bh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1547">007Bh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1548">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1548">007Ch</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1549">007Dh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1549">007Dh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1550">007Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1550">007Eh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1551">007Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1551">007Fh</span></span>     |

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1552">**Nota: le voci con mapping di maiuscole/minuscole senza identità sono in grassetto.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1552">**(Note: entries with non-identity up-case mappings are in bold)**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1553">Durante la formattazione di un volume, le implementazioni possono generare una tabella up-case in un formato compresso usando la compressione del mapping di identità, poiché gran parte dello spazio dei caratteri Unicode non ha alcun concetto di distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole (il che significa che i caratteri "minuscoli" e "maiuscoli" sono equivalenti).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1553">Upon formatting a volume, implementations may generate an up-case table in a compressed format using identity-mapping compression, since a large portion of the Unicode character space has no concept of case (which means the "lower-case" and "upper-case" characters are equivalent).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1554">Le implementazioni comprimeno una tabella up case rappresentando una serie di mapping di identità con il valore FFFFh seguito dal numero di mapping di identità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1554">Implementations compress an up-case table by representing a series of identity mappings with the value FFFFh followed with the number of identity mappings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1555">Ad esempio, un'implementazione può rappresentare i primi mapping di 100 caratteri (64 ore) con le otto voci seguenti di una tabella up case compressa:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1555">For example, an implementation may represent the first 100 (64h) character mappings with the following eight entries of a compressed up-case table:</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1556">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1556">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1557">Le prime due voci indicano che i primi 97 (61h) caratteri (da 0000h a 0060h) hanno mapping di identità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1557">The first two entries indicate the first 97 (61h) characters (from 0000h to 0060h) have identity mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1558">I caratteri successivi, da 0061h a 0063h, vengono mappati rispettivamente ai caratteri da 0041h a 0043h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1558">The subsequent characters, 0061h through 0063h, map to characters 0041h through 0043h, respectively.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1559">La possibilità di fornire una tabella up case compressa al momento della formattazione di un volume è facoltativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1559">The ability to provide a compressed up-case table upon formatting a volume is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1560">Tuttavia, la possibilità di interpretare sia una tabella non compressa che una tabella up-case compressa è obbligatoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1560">However, the ability to interpret both an uncompressed and a compressed up-case table is mandatory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-1561">Il valore del campo TableChecksum è sempre conforme alla modalità di esistenza della tabella up case nel volume, che può essere in formato compresso o non compresso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1561">The value of the TableChecksum field always conforms to how the up-case table exists on the volume, which may be in either compressed or uncompressed format.</span></span>

##### <a name="7251-recommended-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-1562">7.2.5.1 Tabella up case consigliata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1562">7.2.5.1 Recommended Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1563">Quando si formatta un volume, le implementazioni devono registrare la tabella up-case consigliata in formato compresso (vedere la tabella [25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), per cui il valore del campo TableChecksum è E619D30Dh.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1563">When formatting a volume, implementations should record the recommended up-case table in compressed format (see [Table 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), for which the value of the TableChecksum field is E619D30Dh.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-1564">Se un'implementazione definisce la propria tabella up-case, compressa o non compressa, tale tabella dovrà coprire l'intervallo di caratteri Unicode completo (dai codici carattere 0000h a FFFFh inclusi).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-1564">If an implementation defines its own up-case table, either compressed or uncompressed, then that table shall cover the complete Unicode character range (from character codes 0000h to FFFFh inclusive).</span></span>

### <a name="73-volume-label-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4858">7.3 Voce di directory dell'etichetta di volume</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4858">7.3 Volume Label Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4859">L'etichetta di volume è una stringa Unicode che consente agli utenti finali di distinguere i volumi di archiviazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4859">The Volume Label is a Unicode string which enables end users to distinguish their storage volumes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4860">Nella directory exFAT file system l'etichetta di volume esiste come voce di directory primaria critica nella directory radice (vedere [la tabella 26).](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4860">In the exFAT file system, the Volume Label exists as a critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4861">Il numero valido di voci della directory Volume Label è compreso tra 0 e 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4861">The valid number of Volume Label directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

#### <a name="731-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4885">7.3.1 Campo EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4885">7.3.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4886">Il campo EntryType deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello Generic Primary DirectoryEntry (vedere [la sezione 6.3.1).](#631-entrytype-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4886">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1](#631-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7311-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4887">7.3.1.1 Campo TypeCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4887">7.3.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4889">Per la voce di directory Volume Label, il valore valido per questo campo è</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4889">For the Volume Label directory entry, the valid value for this field is</span></span>
3.

##### <a name="7312-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4890">7.3.1.2 Campo TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4890">7.3.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4892">Per la voce di directory Volume Label, il valore valido per questo campo è</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4892">For the Volume Label directory entry, the valid value for this field is</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4896">Il campo InUse deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry primario generico (vedere [la sezione 6.3.1.4).](#6314-inuse-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4896">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.4](#6314-inuse-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="732-charactercount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4897">7.3.2 Campo CharacterCount</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4897">7.3.2 CharacterCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4898">Il campo CharacterCount deve contenere la lunghezza della stringa Unicode contenuta nel campo VolumeLabel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4898">The CharacterCount field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the VolumeLabel field contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4899">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4899">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4900">Almeno 0, il che significa che la stringa Unicode è lunga 0 caratteri (che equivale a nessuna etichetta di volume)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4900">At least 0, which means the Unicode string is 0 characters long (which is the equivalent of no volume label)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4901">Al massimo 11, il che significa che la stringa Unicode è lunga 11 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4901">At most 11, which means the Unicode string is 11 characters long</span></span>

#### <a name="733-volumelabel-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4902">7.3.3 Campo VolumeLabel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4902">7.3.3 VolumeLabel Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4903">Il campo VolumeLabel deve contenere una stringa Unicode, ovvero il nome descrittivo del volume.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4903">The VolumeLabel field shall contain a Unicode string, which is the user-friendly name of the volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4904">Il campo VolumeLabel ha lo stesso set di caratteri non validi del campo FileName della voce di directory File Name (vedere [la sezione 7.7.3).](#773-filename-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4904">The VolumeLabel field has the same set of invalid characters as the FileName field of the File Name directory entry (see [Section 7.7.3](#773-filename-field)).</span></span>

### <a name="74-file-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4905">7.4 Voce della directory dei file</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4905">7.4 File Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4906">Le voci della directory file descrivono file e directory.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4906">File directory entries describe files and directories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4907">Si tratta di voci di directory primarie critiche e qualsiasi directory può contenere zero o più voci di directory file (vedere [la tabella 27).](#table-27-file-directoryentry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4907">They are critical primary directory entries and any directory may contain zero or more File directory entries (see [Table 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-4908">Perché una voce della directory File sia valida, è necessario che almeno una voce della directory Estensione di flusso e almeno una voce di directory Nome file seguano immediatamente la voce della directory File (vedere rispettivamente le sezioni [7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) e [7.7).](#77-file-name-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4908">For a File directory entry to be valid, exactly one Stream Extension directory entry and at least one File Name directory entry must immediately follow the File directory entry (see [Section 7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) and [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="741-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4972">7.4.1 Campo EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4972">7.4.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

##### <a name="7411-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4974">7.4.1.1 Campo TypeCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4974">7.4.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4975">Il campo TypeCode deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry primario generico (vedere [la Sezione 6.3.1.1).](#6311-typecode-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4975">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-4976">Per una voce di directory File, il valore valido per questo campo è 5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4976">For a File directory entry, the valid value for this field is 5.</span></span>

##### <a name="7412-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-4977">7.4.1.2 Campo TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-4977">7.4.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

#### <a name="745-createtimestamp-create10msincrement-and-createutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5025">7.4.5 Campi CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement e CreateUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5025">7.4.5 CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement, and CreateUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5026">In combinazione, i campi CreateTimestamp e CreateTime10msIncrement descrivono la data e l'ora locali in cui è stato creato il file o la directory specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5026">In combination, the CreateTimestamp and CreateTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the given file/directory was created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5027">Il campo CreateUtcOffset descrive l'offset di data e ora locali rispetto all'ora UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5027">The CreateUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5028">Le implementazioni devono impostare questi campi al momento della creazione del set di voci di directory specificato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5028">Implementations shall set these fields upon creation of the given directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5029">Questi campi devono essere conformi alle definizioni dei campi Timestamp, 10msIncrement e UtcOffset (vedere rispettivamente [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)e [Section 7.4.10).](#7410-utcoffset-fields)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5029">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="746-lastmodifiedtimestamp-lastmodified10msincrement-and-lastmodifiedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5030">7.4.6 Campi LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement e LastModifiedUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5030">7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement, and LastModifiedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5031">In combinazione, i campi LastModifiedTimestamp e LastModifiedTime10msIncrement descrivono la data e l'ora locali dell'ultima modifica del contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5031">In combination, the LastModifiedTimestamp and LastModifiedTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5032">Il campo LastModifiedUtcOffset descrive l'offset di data e ora locali rispetto all'ora UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5032">The LastModifiedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5033">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare questi campi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5033">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5034">Dopo aver modificato il contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata (ad eccezione del contenuto che esiste oltre il punto descritto nel campo ValidDataLength)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5034">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the point the ValidDataLength field describes)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5035">Quando si modificano i valori dei campi ValidDataLength o DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5035">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5036">Questi campi devono essere conformi alle definizioni dei campi Timestamp, 10msIncrement e UtcOffset (vedere rispettivamente [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)e [Section 7.4.10).](#7410-utcoffset-fields)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5036">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="747-lastaccessedtimestamp-and-lastaccessedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5037">7.4.7 Campi LastAccessedTimestamp e LastAccessedUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5037">7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp and LastAccessedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5038">Il campo LastAccessedTimestamp deve descrivere la data e l'ora dell'ultimo accesso al contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5038">The LastAccessedTimestamp field shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5039">Il campo LastAccessedUtcOffset descrive l'offset di data e ora locali rispetto all'ora UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5039">The LastAccessedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5040">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare questi campi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5040">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5041">Dopo la modifica del contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata (ad eccezione del contenuto che esiste oltre ValidDataLength)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5041">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the ValidDataLength)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5042">Quando si modificano i valori dei campi ValidDataLength o DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5042">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5043">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare questi campi dopo la lettura del contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5043">Implementations should update these fields after reading the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5044">Questi campi devono essere conformi alle definizioni dei campi Timestamp e UtcOffset (vedere rispettivamente [Sezione 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) e [Sezione 7.4.10).](#7410-utcoffset-fields)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5044">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="748-timestamp-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5045">7.4.8 Campi timestamp</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5045">7.4.8 Timestamp Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5046">I campi timestamp descrivono sia la data locale che l'ora, fino a una risoluzione di due secondi (vedere [la tabella 29).](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5046">Timestamp fields describe both local date and time, down to a two-second resolution (see [Table 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7481-doubleseconds-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5078">7.4.8.1 Campo DoubleSeconds</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5078">7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5079">Il campo DoubleSeconds descrive la parte relativa ai secondi del campo Timestamp, in multipli di due secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5079">The DoubleSeconds field shall describe the seconds portion of the Timestamp field, in two-second multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5080">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5080">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5081">0, che rappresenta 0 secondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5081">0, which represents 0 seconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5082">29, che rappresenta 58 secondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5082">29, which represents 58 seconds</span></span>

##### <a name="7482-minute-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5083">Campo 7.4.8.2 Minute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5083">7.4.8.2 Minute Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5084">Il campo Minute descrive la parte relativa ai minuti del campo Timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5084">The Minute field shall describe the minutes portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5085">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5085">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5086">0, che rappresenta 0 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5086">0, which represents 0 minutes</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5087">59, che rappresenta 59 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5087">59, which represents 59 minutes</span></span>

##### <a name="7483-hour-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5088">Campo 7.4.8.3 Hour</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5088">7.4.8.3 Hour Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5089">Il campo Ora descrive la parte relativa alle ore del campo Timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5089">The Hour field shall describe the hours portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5090">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5090">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5091">0, che rappresenta le ore 00:00</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5091">0, which represents 00:00 hours</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5092">23, che rappresenta le 23:00 ore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5092">23, which represents 23:00 hours</span></span>

##### <a name="7484-day-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5093">Campo 7.4.8.4 Day</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5093">7.4.8.4 Day Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5094">Il campo Giorno descrive la parte relativa al giorno del campo Timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5094">The Day field shall describe the day portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5095">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5095">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5096">1, ovvero il primo giorno del mese specificato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5096">1, which is the first day of the given month</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5097">Ultimo giorno del mese specificato (il mese specificato definisce il numero di giorni validi)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5097">The last day of the given month (the given month defines the number of valid days)</span></span>

##### <a name="7485-month-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5098">7.4.8.5 Campo Month</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5098">7.4.8.5 Month Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5099">Il campo Month deve descrivere la parte relativa al mese del campo Timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5099">The Month field shall describe the month portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5100">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5100">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5101">Almeno 1, che rappresenta gennaio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5101">At least 1, which represents January</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5102">Al massimo 12, che rappresenta dicembre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5102">At most 12, which represents December</span></span>

##### <a name="7486-year-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5103">Campo 7.4.8.6 Year</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5103">7.4.8.6 Year Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5104">Il campo Year deve descrivere la parte relativa all'anno del campo Timestamp, relativa all'anno 1980.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5104">The Year field shall describe the year portion of the Timestamp field, relative to the year 1980.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5105">Questo campo rappresenta l'anno 1980 con il valore 0 e l'anno 2107 con il valore 127.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5105">This field represents the year 1980 with the value 0 and the year 2107 with the value 127.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5106">Tutti i valori possibili per questo campo sono validi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5106">All possible values for this field are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="749-10msincrement-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5107">7.4.9 10msIncrement Fields</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5107">7.4.9 10msIncrement Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5108">I campi 10msIncrement forniscono una risoluzione temporale aggiuntiva ai campi Timestamp corrispondenti in multipli di dieci millisecondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5108">10msIncrement fields shall provide additional time resolution to their corresponding Timestamp fields in ten-millisecond multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5109">L'intervallo valido di valori per questi campi deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5109">The valid range of values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5110">Almeno 0, che rappresenta 0 millisecondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5110">At least 0, which represents 0 milliseconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5111">Al massimo 199, che rappresenta 1990 millisecondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5111">At most 199, which represents 1990 milliseconds</span></span>

#### <a name="7410-utcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5112">7.4.10 Campi UtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5112">7.4.10 UtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5113">I campi UtcOffset (vedere la tabella [30)](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)descrivono l'offset dall'ora UTC alla data e all'ora locali che descrivono i campi Timestamp e 10msIncrement corrispondenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5113">UtcOffset fields (see [Table 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) shall describe the offset from UTC to the local date and time their corresponding Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields describe.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5114">L'offset dall'ora UTC alla data e all'ora locali include gli effetti dei fusi orari e di altre modifiche di data e ora, ad esempio l'ora legale e le variazioni dell'ora legale a livello di area.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5114">The offset from UTC to the local date and time includes the effects of time zones and other date-time adjustments, such as daylight saving and regional summer time changes.</span></span>

<div id="table-30-utcoffset-field-structure" />

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5115">**Tabella 30 Struttura del campo UtcOffset**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5115">**Table 30 UtcOffset Field Structure**</span></span>

<table>

##### <a name="74101-offsetfromutc-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5130">7.4.10.1 Campo OffsetFromUtc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5130">7.4.10.1 OffsetFromUtc Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5131">Il campo OffsetFromUtc descrive l'offset dall'ora UTC della data e dell'ora locali contenute nei campi Timestamp e 10msIncrement correlati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5131">The OffsetFromUtc field shall describe the offset from UTC of the local date and time the related Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields contains.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5132">Questo campo descrive l'offset dall'ora UTC a intervalli di 15 minuti (vedere la tabella 31).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5132">This field describes the offset from UTC in 15 minute intervals (see Table 31).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5176">Come indicato nella tabella precedente, tutti i valori possibili per questo campo sono validi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5176">As the table above indicates, all possible values for this field are valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5177">Tuttavia, le implementazioni devono registrare solo il valore 00h per questo campo quando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5177">However, implementations should only record the value 00h for this field when:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5178">La data e l'ora locali sono in realtà uguali all'ora UTC, nel qual caso il valore del campo OffsetValid deve essere 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5178">Local date and time are actually the same as UTC, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5179">La data e l'ora locali non sono note, nel qual caso il valore del campo OffsetValid deve essere 1 e le implementazioni considerino l'ora UTC come data e ora locali</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5179">Local date and time are not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1 and implementations shall consider UTC to be local date and time</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5180">UTC non è noto, nel qual caso il valore del campo OffsetValid deve essere 0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5180">UTC is not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 0</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5181">Se la differenza di data e ora locale dall'ora UTC non è un multiplo di intervalli di 15 minuti, le implementazioni registrano 00h nel campo OffsetFromUtc e considerano UTC come data e ora locali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5181">If the local date and time offset from UTC happens to not be a multiple of 15 minute intervals, then implementations shall record 00h in the OffsetFromUtc field and shall consider UTC to be local date and time.</span></span>

##### <a name="74102-offsetvalid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5182">7.4.10.2 Campo OffsetValid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5182">7.4.10.2 OffsetValid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5183">Il campo OffsetValid deve indicare se il contenuto del campo OffsetFromUtc è valido o meno, come indicato di seguito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5183">The OffsetValid field shall describe whether the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid or not, as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5184">0, ovvero il contenuto del campo OffsetFromUtc non è valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5184">0, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are invalid</span></span>
    > <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5185">e devono essere 00h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5185">and shall be 00h</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5186">1, ovvero il contenuto del campo OffsetFromUtc è valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5186">1, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5187">Le implementazioni devono impostare questo campo sul valore 0 solo quando l'ora UTC non è disponibile per il calcolo del valore del campo OffsetFromUtc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5187">Implementations should only set this field to the value 0 when UTC is not available for computing the value of the OffsetFromUtc field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5188">Se questo campo contiene il valore 0, le implementazioni devono considerare i campi Timestamp e 10msIncrement come con lo stesso offset UTC della data e dell'ora locali correnti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5188">If this field contains the value 0, then implementations shall treat the Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields as having the same UTC offset as the current local date and time.</span></span>

### <a name="75-volume-guid-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5189">7.5 Voce di directory GUID volume</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5189">7.5 Volume GUID Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5190">La voce di directory GUID volume contiene un GUID che consente alle implementazioni di distinguere i volumi in modo univoco e a livello di codice.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5190">The Volume GUID directory entry contains a GUID which enables implementations to uniquely and programmatically distinguish volumes.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5191">Il GUID del volume esiste come voce di directory primaria non dannosa nella directory radice (vedere [la tabella 32).](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5191">The Volume GUID exists as a benign primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5192">Il numero valido di voci di directory GUID del volume è compreso tra 0 e 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5192">The valid number of Volume GUID directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5254">Inoltre, questa voce di directory è valida solo se segue immediatamente la voce della directory File.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5254">Further, this directory entry is valid only if it immediately follows the File directory entry.</span></span>

#### <a name="762-generalsecondaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5314">7.6.2 Campo GeneralSecondaryFlags</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5314">7.6.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5315">Il campo GeneralSecondaryFlags deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere la sezione [6.4.2)](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)e definisce il contenuto del campo CustomDefined da riservare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5315">The GeneralSecondaryFlags field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) and defines the contents of the CustomDefined field to be reserved.</span></span>

##### <a name="7621-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5316">7.6.2.1 Campo AllocationPossible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5316">7.6.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5317">Il campo AllocationPossible deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere [la sezione 6.4.2.1).](#6421-allocationpossible-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5317">The AllocationPossible field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5318">Per la voce di directory Estensione flusso, il valore valido per questo campo è 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5318">For the Stream Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="7622-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5319">7.6.2.2 Campo NoFatChain</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5319">7.6.2.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5320">Il campo NoFatChain deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere [la sezione 6.4.2.2).](#6422-nofatchain-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5320">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="763-namelength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5321">7.6.3 Campo NameLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5321">7.6.3 NameLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5322">Il campo NameLength deve contenere la lunghezza della stringa Unicode contenuta collettivamente nelle voci successive della directory Nome file (vedere la sezione [7.7).](#77-file-name-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5322">The NameLength field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the subsequent File Name directory entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) collectively contain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5323">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5323">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5324">Almeno 1, ovvero il nome file più breve possibile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5324">At least 1, which is the shortest possible file name</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5325">Al massimo 255, ovvero il nome file più lungo possibile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5325">At most 255, which is the longest possible file name</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5326">Il valore del campo NameLength influisce anche sul numero di voci di directory nome file (vedere [la sezione 7.7).](#77-file-name-directory-entry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5326">The value of the NameLength field also affects the number File Name Directory Entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span>

#### <a name="764-namehash-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5327">7.6.4 Campo NameHash</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5327">7.6.4 NameHash Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5328">Il campo NameHash deve contenere un hash a 2 byte (vedere [la figura 4)](#figure-4-namehash-computation)del nome del file con distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5328">The NameHash field shall contain a 2-byte hash (see [Figure 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation)) of the up-cased file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5329">Ciò consente alle implementazioni di eseguire un confronto rapido durante la ricerca di un file in base al nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5329">This enables implementations to perform a quick comparison when searching for a file by name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5330">È importante notare che NameHash fornisce una verifica sicura di una mancata corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5330">Importantly, the NameHash provides a sure verification of a mismatch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5331">Le implementazioni devono verificare tutte le corrispondenze nameHash con un confronto del nome file con distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5331">Implementations shall verify all NameHash matches with a comparison of the up-cased file name.</span></span>

<div id="figure-4-namehash-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5332">**Figura 4 Calcolo NameHash**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5332">**Figure 4 NameHash Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt16 NameHash
(
    WCHAR * FileName,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-cased file name
    UCHAR   NameLength
)
{
    UCHAR  * Buffer = (UCHAR *)FileName;
    UInt16   NumberOfBytes = (UInt16)NameLength * 2;
    UInt16   Hash = 0;
    UInt16   Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        Hash = ((Hash&1) ? 0x8000 : 0) + (Hash>>1) + (UInt16)Buffer[Index];
    }
    return Hash;
}
```

#### <a name="765-validdatalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5333">7.6.5 Campo ValidDataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5333">7.6.5 ValidDataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5334">Il campo ValidDataLength deve descrivere quanto sono stati scritti i dati utente del flusso di dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5334">The ValidDataLength field shall describe how far into the data stream user data has been written.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5335">Le implementazioni aggiorneranno questo campo mentre scrivono i dati nel flusso di dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5335">Implementations shall update this field as they write data further out into the data stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5336">Nei supporti di archiviazione i dati compresi tra la lunghezza dei dati valida e la lunghezza del flusso di dati non sono definiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5336">On the storage media, the data between the valid data length and the data length of the data stream is undefined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5337">Le implementazioni restituiranno zeri per le operazioni di lettura oltre la lunghezza dei dati valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5337">Implementations shall return zeroes for read operations beyond the valid data length.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5338">Se la voce di directory File corrispondente descrive una directory, l'unico valore valido per questo campo è uguale al valore del campo DataLength.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5338">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the only valid value for this field is equal to the value of the DataLength field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5339">In caso contrario, l'intervallo di valori validi per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5339">Otherwise, the range of valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5340">Almeno 0, ovvero nessun dato utente è stato scritto nel flusso di dati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5340">At least 0, which means no user data has been written out to the data stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5341">Al massimo DataLength, il che significa che i dati utente sono stati scritti per l'intera lunghezza del flusso di dati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5341">At most DataLength, which means user data has been written out to the entire length of the data stream</span></span>

#### <a name="766-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5342">7.6.6 Campo FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5342">7.6.6 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5343">Il campo FirstCluster deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere [la sezione 6.4.3).](#643-firstcluster-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5343">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.3](#643-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5344">Questo campo deve contenere l'indice del primo cluster del flusso di dati, che ospita i dati utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5344">This field shall contain the index of the first cluster of the data stream, which hosts the user data.</span></span>

#### <a name="767-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5345">7.6.7 Campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5345">7.6.7 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5347">Se la voce di directory File corrispondente descrive una directory, il valore valido per questo campo corrisponde all'intera dimensione dell'allocazione associata, in byte, che può essere 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5347">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the valid value for this field is the entire size of the associated allocation, in bytes, which may be 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5348">Inoltre, per le directory, il valore massimo per questo campo è 256 MB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5348">Further, for directories, the maximum value for this field is 256MB.</span></span>

### <a name="77-file-name-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5349">7.7 Voce di directory nome file</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5349">7.7 File Name Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5350">Le voci della directory Nome file sono voci di directory secondarie critiche nei set di voci della directory file (vedere [la tabella 34).](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5350">File Name directory entries are critical secondary directory entries in File directory entry sets (see [Table 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5351">Il numero valido di voci di directory File Name in un set di voci della directory File è NameLength/ 15, arrotondato per esere all'intero più vicino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5351">The valid number of File Name directory entries in a File directory entry set is NameLength / 15, rounded up to the nearest integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5352">Inoltre, le voci di directory Nome file sono valide solo se seguono immediatamente la voce di directory Estensione di flusso come serie consecutive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5352">Further, File Name directory entries are valid only if they immediately follow the Stream Extension directory entry as a consecutive series.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5353">Le voci della directory Nome file vengono combinate in modo da formare il nome file per il set di voci della directory File.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5353">File Name directory entries combine to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5354">Tutti gli elementi figlio di una determinata voce di directory devono avere set di voci di directory nome file univoci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5354">All children of a given directory entry shall have unique File Name Directory Entry Sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5355">Ciò significa che non possono essere presenti nomi di file o directory duplicati dopo l'up-casing all'interno di una directory.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5355">That is to say there can be no duplicate file or directory names after up-casing within any one directory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5393">Il campo NoFatChain deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere [la Sezione 6.4.2.2).](#6422-nofatchain-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5393">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="773-filename-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5394">7.7.3 Campo FileName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5394">7.7.3 FileName Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5395">Il campo FileName deve contenere una stringa Unicode, ovvero una parte del nome file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5395">The FileName field shall contain a Unicode string, which is a portion of the file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5396">Nell'ordine in cui le voci di directory File Name sono presenti in un set di voci di directory File, i campi FileName vengono concatenati per formare il nome file per il set di voci della directory File.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5396">In the order File Name directory entries exist in a File directory entry set, FileName fields concatenate to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5397">Data la lunghezza del campo FileName, 15 caratteri e il numero massimo di voci di directory File Name, 17, la lunghezza massima del nome file concatenato finale è 17.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5397">Given the length of the FileName field, 15 characters, and the maximum number of File Name directory entries, 17, the maximum length of the final, concatenated file name is</span></span>
255.

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5398">Il nome file concatenato ha lo stesso set di caratteri non validi degli altri file system basati su FAT (vedere [la tabella 35).](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5398">The concatenated file name has the same set of illegal characters as other FAT-based file systems (see [Table 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5399">Le implementazioni devono impostare i caratteri inutilizzati dei campi FileName sul valore 0000h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5399">Implementations should set the unused characters of FileName fields to the value 0000h.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5473">002Ah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5473">002Ah</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5474">Asterisco</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5474">Asterisk</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5475">002Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5475">002Fh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5476">Barra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5476">Forward slash</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5477">003Ah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5477">003Ah</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5478">Due punti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5478">Colon</span></span>           |
| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5479">003Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5479">003Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5480">Segno di minore a</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5480">Less-than sign</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5481">003Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5481">003Eh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5482">Segno di maggiore di</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5482">Greater-than sign</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5483">003Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5483">003Fh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5484">Punto interrogativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5484">Question mark</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5485">005Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5485">005Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5486">Barra rovesciata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5486">Back slash</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5487">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5487">007Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5488">Barra verticale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5488">Vertical bar</span></span>      |                    |                 |

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5489">I nomi di file "." e ".." hanno rispettivamente il significato speciale di "questa directory" e "directory contenitore".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5489">The file names "." and ".." have the special meaning of "this directory" and "containing directory", respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5490">Le implementazioni non devono registrare uno di questi nomi di file riservati nel campo FileName.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5490">Implementations shall not record either of these reserved file names in the FileName field.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5491">Tuttavia, le implementazioni possono generare questi due nomi di file negli elenchi di directory per fare riferimento alla directory elencata e alla directory contenitore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5491">However, implementations may generate these two file names in directory listings to refer to the directory being listed and the containing directory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5492">Le implementazioni possono voler limitare i nomi di file e directory solo al set di caratteri ASCII.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5492">Implementations may wish to restrict file and directory names to just the ASCII character set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5493">In tal caso, è necessario limitare l'utilizzo dei caratteri all'intervallo di caratteri validi nelle prime 128 voci Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5493">If so they should limit their character use to the range of valid characters in the first 128 Unicode entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5494">Devono comunque archiviare i nomi di file e directory in Unicode nel volume e convertirsi in/da ASCII/Unicode durante l'interfacciamento con l'utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5494">They must still store file and directory names in Unicode on the volume and translate to/from ASCII/Unicode when interfacing with the user.</span></span>

### <a name="78-vendor-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5495">7.8 Voce della directory dell'estensione del fornitore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5495">7.8 Vendor Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5496">La voce di directory Vendor Extension è una voce di directory secondaria non dannosa nei set di voci della directory File (vedere [la tabella 36).](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5496">The Vendor Extension directory entry is a benign secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5497">Un set di voci della directory File può contenere un numero qualsiasi di voci di directory vendor extension, fino al limite di voci di directory secondarie, meno il numero di altre voci di directory secondarie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5497">A File directory entry set may contain any number of Vendor Extension directory entries, up to the limit of secondary directory entries, less the number of other secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5498">Inoltre, le voci della directory Vendor Extension sono valide solo se non precedono le voci di directory Stream Extension e File Name obbligatorie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5498">Further, Vendor Extension directory entries are valid only if they do not precede the required Stream Extension and File Name directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5499">Le voci della directory Vendor Extension consentono ai fornitori di avere voci di directory univoche specifiche del fornitore nei singoli set di voci della directory File tramite il campo VendorGuid (vedere [la tabella 36).](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5499">Vendor Extension directory entries enable vendors to have unique, vendor-specific directory entries in individual File directory entry sets via the VendorGuid field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5500">Le voci di directory univoche consentono ai fornitori di estendere in modo efficace il file system exFAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5500">Unique directory entries effectively enable vendors to extend the exFAT file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5501">I fornitori possono definire il contenuto del campo VendorDefined (Vedere [la tabella 36).](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5501">Vendors may define the contents of the VendorDefined field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9b877-5502">Le implementazioni del fornitore possono mantenere il contenuto del campo VendorDefined e possono fornire funzionalità specifiche del fornitore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5502">Vendor implementations may maintain the contents of the VendorDefined field and may provide vendor-specific functionality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5503">Le implementazioni che non riconoscono il GUID di una voce di directory dell'estensione fornitore devono considerare la voce di directory come qualsiasi altra voce di directory secondaria non riconosciuta non riconosciuta (vedere la sezione [8.2).](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5503">Implementations which do not recognize the GUID of a Vendor Extension directory entry shall treat the directory entry the same as any other unrecognized benign secondary directory entry (see [Section 8.2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span></span>

#### <a name="781-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5527">7.8.1 Campo EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5527">7.8.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5528">Il campo EntryType deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere [la sezione 6.4.1).](#641-entrytype-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5528">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1](#641-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7811-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5529">7.8.1.1 Campo TypeCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5529">7.8.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5530">Il campo TypeCode deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere [la sezione 6.4.1.1).](#6411-typecode-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5530">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.1](#6411-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9b877-5531">Per la voce di directory Vendor Extension il valore valido per questo campo è 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5531">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7812-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5532">7.8.1.2 Campo TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5532">7.8.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

##### <a name="7814-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="9b877-5537">7.8.1.4 Campo InUse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9b877-5537">7.8.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>
